| 2026-05-17 | **Phase Q17 9B-6 HOTFIX ÔÇö freshly drawn stair flickered in then disappeared**. Two-part fix: (a) `useStairPersistence` diff-merge now preserves local stairs that have never been persisted (`!lastSavedParamsRef.current.has(id)`) in addition to in-flight dirty stairs. Without this guard, a stair placed via the tool was added to the local scene, then the next Firestore snapshot fired before `floorplan_stairs/{id}` round-tripped ÔÇö the diff-merge saw "in scene but not in docs" and dropped it (mutated=true Ôćĺ scene rewritten without the stair). (b) `onStairCreated` in `useSpecialTools` now emits `EventBus.emit('drawing:entity-created', { entity, tool: 'stair' })` (event slot existed in `EventBus.ts` but was unused); `useStairPersistence` subscribes and triggers `persist(entity)` immediately so the first save fires without requiring the user to select + edit the new stair. Pairs with the diff-merge preserve so the optimistic local entity survives until the save completes, then the snapshot picks up the persisted doc cleanly. Industry pattern 5/5 (Revit transaction commit + Firestore optimistic UI + Google Docs immediate-save). Zero new state, two-file fix (~16 LOC). |

| 2026-05-17 | **Phase 9B-2 IMPLEMENTED ÔÇö strict floor-bound stair mode (Q35)**. NEW SSoT module `systems/stairs/stair-floor-link.ts` (`reconcileLinkedStair` pure + idempotent, `maxStepCountFor` / `minStepCountFor` code-aware bounds, `deriveRiseFromStepCount` inverse, exported `mmFactorFromWidth` heuristic) ÔÇö Tier-3 candidate; existing `mmFactorFromWidth` copies in `stair-validator` / `stair-auto-fix` / `stair-grips` remain for now (TODO follow-up to consolidate via `resolveSceneUnits` SSoT, ADR-358 Phase 8). `useRibbonStairBridge` patch helpers wire reconcile: `patchRise` calls `reconcileLinkedStair(withRecomputedTotals(...))` so rise is the primary lever; `patchStepCount` inverts when linked (`deriveRiseFromStepCount` Ôćĺ rewrite rise Ôćĺ reconcile) so stepCount lands exactly on the envelope (Revit "Desired Riser Height" pattern). `stair-grips.resizeLength` clamps the length grip to `tread ├Ś (maxStepCount Ôłĺ 1)` (scene units) and magnet-snaps at the last 10% of `maxRun` (Revit / ArchiCAD "magnet to top level"); `totalRise` is locked to `storyHeight ├Ś storyCount`. `stair-completion.buildDefaultStairParams` reconciles post-build so a stair placed on a 3000mm floor with default 175mm rise lands on `stepCount = 17` out of the box (instead of seeded 12). `stair-validator.checkStoryHeightOverflow` + `checkStoryHeightUnderflow` emit `hardError.totalRiseOverFloor` / `hardError.totalRiseUnderFloor` when linked (red box) instead of the soft `totalRiseOver/BelowStoryHeight` (orange); both are appended to the `hardErrors` field so `StairWarningsSection.partitionViolations` routes them correctly. `stair-auto-fix.autoFixStairParams` reconciles BEFORE the code-range fixes so "Auto-fix" on a linked stair never reintroduces overflow. Stringers `inner` + `outer` = constant-R polylines sampled at the same `stepCount+1` angular grid (R=innerRadius and R=outerRadius respectively). cutLine = `buildCutLine` from shared, passed a degenerate 4-vertex tread at the mid-radius of the first tread crossing the cut plane + the local tangent vector `(-sign┬Ěsin ╬Ş, sign┬Ěcos ╬Ş)` as `uDir` Ôćĺ cut spans the wedge width perpendicular to walkline direction. Apex-at-center degenerate helical: `innerRadius=0` fixed by type, treads are triangular wedges (3 vertices: `apex, outerA, outerB` ccw; mirrored vertex order for cw). Outer radius = `params.width` (industry convention for central-column spiral stairs). Walkline reuses Phase 2a `helixSample(centerPoint, 0, width, ÔÇŽ)` ÔÇö degenerate inner radius reduces to walkline at R=width/2 sampled uniform-angular. Risers vertical at outer corner of ╬Ş_{i+1}. Stringers: `outer` = polyline at R=width, `inner` = `stepCount+1` copies of `centerPoint(z_i)` (no inner stringer for column-less spiral by type contract ÔÇö preserves StairStringerGeometry shape). cutLine same pattern as helical. (3) **EDIT** `systems/stairs/StairGeometryService.ts` ÔÇö dispatch `'spiral'` Ôćĺ `computeSpiral`, `'helical'` Ôćĺ `computeHelical` replaces Phase 4a sentinel throws; exhaustive `never` guard preserved on Phase 4b/4c kinds. (5) **NEW** `__tests__/StairGeometryService-helical.test.ts` (10 test) ÔÇö stepCount=12, sweep=270┬░, innerRadius=400, outerRadius=1400, ccw: 4-vertex wedge per tread; z=i┬Ěrise co-planar; inner corners at R=400 / outer at R=1400; angular increment 22.5┬░ (cos/sin compare); walkline 13 vertices all at R=900 = (400+1400)/2; total chord length Ôëł stepCount┬Ě2R┬Ěsin(╬ö╬Ş/2) analytical (tol 1e-3 for piecewise-linear approximation of a circular arc); inner stringer 13 vertices at R=400 / outer 13 vertices at R=1400; cw mirrors ccw across x-axis; cutLine emitted for totalRise=2100 / undefined for rise=50; treadLabels 'all' Ôćĺ 12 labels at tread centroids. **20/20 Phase 4a green** + **74/74 cumulative stairs** + **240/240 cumulative geometry-shared regression green** (~6s). | 2026-05-16 | **Phase 4b IMPLEMENTED** ÔÇö `StairGeometryService` kind `elliptical` + `winder` operativi (`winderMethod Ôłł {'equal-going','pie'}`; `'kite'`/`'balanced'` Phase 4c sentinel). 5 file (2 new + 1 service edit + 2 new test): (1) **NEW** `systems/stairs/stair-geometry-elliptical.ts` (~165 LOC) ÔÇö `computeElliptical(params, variant: StairVariantElliptical)`. Walkline = Phase 2b `ellipseSample(centerPoint, semiMajor, semiMinor, sweepAngle, turnDirection, rotation, stepCount, totalRise)` directly (stepCount+1 points along arc-length parameterized ellipse perimeter, rotated by `rotation`). Treads: 4-vertex polygon per step extending ┬▒`width/2` to either side of walkline along local chord-perpendicular (industry-standard chord-tangent offset for stair on curved walkline ÔÇö same convention as Revit/ArchiCAD/Vectorworks; NOT a true ellipse offset which is non-elliptical and would require Clipper-class machinery, error imperceptible for stair widths Ôë¬ semi-axes). Vertex order `[innerA, outerA, outerB, innerB]` for ccw (sign=+1), reversed for cw. Risers vertical at inner corner of tread boundary i+1, using next-tread chord-perpendicular for consistency. Stringers via shared `buildStringersFromWalkline` (offsetPolyline). cutLine: chord-tangent perpendicular at first walkline segment crossing cutPlaneHeight, mid-segment xy. (2) **NEW** `systems/stairs/stair-geometry-winder.ts` (~275 LOC) ÔÇö `computeWinder(params, variant: StairVariantWinder)`. Three-zone layout: flight 1 (n1 rectilinear) Ôćĺ winder zone (winderCount wedges) Ôćĺ flight 2 (n2 rectilinear). `n1 = floor((stepCountÔłĺwinderCount)/2)`, `n2 = remainder`. Pivot = `basePoint + u1┬Ě(n1┬Ětread) + v1┬Ě(turnSign┬ĚhalfW)` (inner side of L turn). u2 = rotate(u1, turnAngle┬ĚDEG2RAD). Winder rays: ray_0 = `-turnSign┬Ěv1`, ray_j = rotate(ray_0, j┬ĚsignedSweepRad), signedSweepRad = turnAngle┬ĚDEG2RAD / winderCount. Outer radius of winder wedges = `params.width`. 'equal-going' treads = 4-vertex `[apex, outerA, outerB, apex]` (sign=+1) or reversed (sign=-1) ÔÇö degenerate inner edge collapsed at pivot, centroid-friendly for labels. 'pie' treads = 3-vertex `[apex, outerA, outerB]`. z model: tread i at z=i┬Ěrise for ALL treads (no landing insertion). Risers within straight flights only (winder risers degenerate at pivot). Flight 2 origin = pivot; width axis = ray_winderCount (= trailing winder boundary direction: 90┬░ Ôćĺ u1, 180┬░ Ôćĺ ┬▒v1). Walkline 1+winderCount+1+(n2>0 ? 1 : 0) vertices: basePoint Ôćĺ winder samples (j=0..winderCount at radius `halfW` from pivot, z linear) Ôćĺ flight 2 end. Stringers via shared `buildStringersFromWalkline` (offsetPolyline handles miter at all winder sample joints). cutLine via shared `buildCutLineForFlights([n1, winderCount, n2], [u1, midWinderTangent, u2], ÔÇŽ)` ÔÇö midWinderTangent = perp_signed(ray_mid) preserves turnSign convention. (3) **EDIT** `systems/stairs/StairGeometryService.ts` ÔÇö dispatch `'elliptical'` Ôćĺ `computeElliptical`, `'winder'` Ôćĺ `computeWinder` replaces Phase 4b sentinel throws; exhaustive `never` guard preserved on Phase 4c kinds (`triangular-fan`/`triangular-outline`/`sketch`). | 2026-05-16 | **Phase 4c IMPLEMENTED** ÔÇö `StairGeometryService` kind `triangular-fan` + `triangular-outline` + `sketch` operativi (Phase 4c sentinel rimosso, dispatch completo per gli ultimi 3 kind della discriminated union ÔÇö solo `winderMethod Ôłł {'kite','balanced'}` resta sentinel deferito a sub-phase futura). 7 file (3 new computers + 1 service edit + 3 new test files): (1) **NEW** `systems/stairs/stair-geometry-triangular-fan.ts` (~200 LOC) ÔÇö `computeTriangularFan(params, variant: StairVariantTriangularFan)`. Apex-at-`apexPoint` polygonal fan/wedge stair (industry: Allplan/AutoCAD Arch "fan stair"). Riusa Phase 2a `helixSample(apexPoint, 0, params.width, openingAngle, turnDirection, stepCount, totalRise)` per walkline (inner=0 Ôçĺ walkline radius = width/2; ZERO duplicate trig). Treads 3-vertex `[apex, outerA, outerB]` (sign=+1 ccw) o `[apex, outerB, outerA]` (sign=-1 cw) ÔÇö simmetria semantica con spiral. Outer radius = `params.width`. Risers vertical at outer corner di ╬Ş_{i+1}. Stringers: outer = polyline at R=width sampled uniform-angular (stepCount+1 punti); inner = stepCount+1 copie di `apexPoint(z_i)` (degenerate, come spiral). cutLine pattern identico a spiral (tangent perp al radial, mid-radius). (2) **NEW** `systems/stairs/stair-geometry-triangular-outline.ts` (~190 LOC) ÔÇö `computeTriangularOutline(params, variant: StairVariantTriangularOutline)`. Wedge stair che riempie footprint triangolare (industry: Vectorworks "Vertex mode", Allplan "triangular landing"). Entry side `triangleVertices[entrySide]ÔćĺtriangleVertices[(entrySide+1)%3]`; apex `triangleVertices[(entrySide+2)%3]`. Equal-height linear slices PARALLEL all'entry edge, ascendenti verso l'apex. Per tread i: corners low_a/low_b at `t_i=i/stepCount` (= V_a+t_i┬Ě(V_c-V_a), V_b+t_i┬Ě(V_c-V_b)); high_a/high_b at `t_{i+1}=(i+1)/stepCount`. Ultimo tread degenera a triangolo all'apex (high_a===high_b===V_c, polygon `[low_a, low_b, V_c, V_c]`). Vertex order: ccw `[low_a, low_b, high_b, high_a]` / cw `[low_a, high_a, high_b, low_b]`. Walkline da midpoint entry edge `(V_a+V_b)/2` Ôćĺ apex `V_c`, stepCount+1 vertices, z linear `i┬Ěrise`. Risers vertical at corner low_a del tread i+1 (= sull'edge V_a-V_c). Stringers via shared `buildStringersFromWalkline(walkline, width)` ÔÇö accept offsetPolyline su retta semplice (no special-case needed). cutLine via shared `buildCutLine` con `axis = normalize(V_c - entryMid)`. `orientation` Ôłł {'cw','ccw'} flippa winding polygon coerentemente con helical/elliptical. | 2026-05-16 | **Phase 5c IMPLEMENTED** ÔÇö Stair Transforms G17 (mirror / rotate / copy) operativi come pure functions, anti-Revit-bug auto-flip (Q23). **2 file** (1 NEW prod + 1 NEW test): **NEW (1)** `systems/stairs/stair-transforms.ts` (~250 LOC) ÔÇö tre public pure functions `mirrorStairParams(params, axisStart, axisEnd)`, `rotateStairParams(params, pivot, angleDeg)`, `copyStairParams(params, delta)`. Tutte ritornano `StairParams` (zero React, zero command, zero Firestore ÔÇö Phase 5c.1 deferita per branch in standard `MirrorEntityCommand`/`RotateEntityCommand`/`MoveEntityCommand`). SSoT riusati: `utils/mirror-math` (`mirrorPoint`/`mirrorAngle`/`getAxisAngleDeg`/`MirrorAxis`) per reflection 2D, `utils/rotation-math` (`rotatePoint`) per rotation 2D, `geometry-utils.normalizeAngleDeg` per angle wrap. Internal helpers (`mirrorPoint3D`/`rotatePoint3D`/`translatePoint3D`) lift Point2D math al 3D preservando `z` (xy-plane transforms, z immutato). Dispatch per `variant.kind` con 3 funzioni esaustive (`mirrorVariant`/`rotateVariant`/`copyVariant`) ciascuna con `never` guard nel default ÔÇö coverage discriminata su tutte 11 kind `straight`/`l-shape`/`u-shape`/`gamma`/`spiral`/`helical`/`elliptical`/`winder`/`triangular-fan`/`triangular-outline`/`sketch`. **Q23 auto-flip semantics**: mirror inverte `turnDirection` LR (`l-shape`/`u-shape` `'left'Ôćö'right'`) e CW (`spiral`/`helical`/`elliptical`/`triangular-fan` `'cw'Ôćö'ccw'`), per `gamma` flippa ogni entry di `turnSequence`, per `triangular-outline` flippa `orientation` CW, per `winder` negate `turnAngle` (signed angle, sign indica direction); `elliptical.rotation` mirrored via `mirrorAngle(rotation, axisAngleDeg)`; variant-internal points (`centerPoint`/`apexPoint`/`triangleVertices`/`walklinePath`) tutti reflected. Rotate: `basePoint` rotato around pivot, `direction += angleDeg`, `elliptical.rotation += angleDeg`, variant-internal points ruotati, `turnDirection`/`turnSequence` invariati (rotation preserves chirality). Copy: solo translate `basePoint` + variant-internal points, `direction`/`turnDirection`/`turnSequence` invariati. Idempotency garantita: `mirror Ôłś mirror Ôëí identity` (test esplicito tol 1e-6), `rotate(0┬░) Ôëí identity`, `copy({0,0}) Ôëí identity`. **NEW (2)** `systems/stairs/__tests__/stair-transforms.test.ts` (~340 LOC, 27 test): mirror X axis (yÔćĺ-y, dir 30┬░Ôćĺ330┬░), mirror Y axis (xÔćĺ-x, dir 30┬░Ôćĺ150┬░), mirror y=x diagonal (a,b)Ôćĺ(b,a), mirror l-shape `rightÔćĺleft`, mirror gamma `['right','left']Ôćĺ['left','right']`, mirror spiral cwÔćĺccw + centerPoint reflected, mirror helical radii preserved, mirror elliptical rotation 30┬░Ôćĺ330┬░ + centerPoint reflected, mirror winder turnAngle 90Ôćĺ-90, mirror triangular-outline vertices + orientation flipped, mirror sketch walkline z preserved, mirror twice Ôëí identity per spiral con tilted axis (1,2)-(5,3); rotate basePoint 90┬░/180┬░/-45┬░, rotate spiral centerPoint preserves turnDirection, rotate elliptical rotation 30+60=90┬░, rotate triangular-outline ogni vertex, rotate triangular-fan apexPoint, rotate sketch z preserved, rotate(0┬░) identity; copy translate basePoint, copy spiral centerPoint, copy gamma turnSequence unchanged, copy triangular-outline ogni vertex, copy({0,0}) identity. **27/27 nuovi test green** (+27 sopra cumulative Phase 5b 152) Ôćĺ **179/179 cumulative** stairs+drawing+commands (~4s isolato). LOC: ~250 prod + ~340 test = ~590 totale (entrambi file ben sotto 500-LOC GOL ceiling per i file di prod). SSoT verifiche: ZERO duplicate reflection math (`mirrorPoint`/`mirrorAngle`/`getAxisAngleDeg` da `utils/mirror-math`); ZERO duplicate rotation math (`rotatePoint` da `utils/rotation-math`); ZERO duplicate angle normalization (`normalizeAngleDeg` da `geometry-utils`); types reused (`StairParams`/`StairVariantParams`/`StairTurnDirectionLR`/`StairTurnDirectionCW` da Phase 1 `types/stair.ts`, `Point2D`/`Point3D` da `rendering/types/Types`); nessuna nuova entry in `.ssot-registry.json` necessaria ÔÇö modulo gi├á pre-registrato in ┬ž11/13 list of post-merge follow-up moduli. Panel inserted between `stair-multistory` and `stair-actions`. flight3 combobox no-ops for l-shape/u-shape (gamma-only via discriminated-union patch helper). **EDIT (16)** `src/subapps/dxf-viewer/ui/ribbon/components/RibbonBody.tsx` ÔÇö read `getPanelVisibility` from `useRibbonCommand()` context + `.filter(p => p.visibilityKey === undefined || getPanelVisibility(p.visibilityKey))` upstream of both `isSettingsMode` and normal-mode panel maps. **i18n** (2 file): **EDIT (17+18)** `src/i18n/locales/{el,en}/dxf-viewer-settings.json` ÔÇö `dynamicInput.placeholders.{rise,tread,stairWidth}` ("¤Ç.¤ç. 175" / "¤Ç.¤ç. 280" / "¤Ç.¤ç. 1200"). **EDIT (19+20)** `src/i18n/locales/{el,en}/dxf-viewer-shell.json` ÔÇö `ribbon.panels.stairMultiFlight` (Greek "╬á╬┐╬╗╬╗╬▒¤Ç╬╗╬Č ╬ú╬║╬ş╬╗╬Ě", English "Multi-Flight") + `ribbon.commands.stairEditor.{flight2TurnDirection,flight3TurnDirection,turnDirectionLeft,turnDirectionRight}` (Greek pure: "╬ú¤ä¤ü╬┐¤ć╬« ╬ú╬║╬ş╬╗╬┐¤ů¤é 2/3 / ╬Ĺ¤ü╬╣¤â¤ä╬Á¤ü╬Č / ╬ö╬Á╬ż╬╣╬Č", English: "Flight 2/3 Turn / Left / Right"). **N.7.2 Google-level checklist**: Ôťů proactive (Dynamic Input rise/tread/width visible immediately on tool activation, no cursor-position prerequisite ÔÇö industry pre-set workflow); Ôťů no race (Stream E `confirmWithOverrides` bypasses React setState batching by applying overrides atomically inside `commitFromState`; Stream F panel visibility is pure read from current variant.kind at render time, no stale state); Ôťů idempotent (Stream E onChange normalize commas to dots, Tab cycle is pure ring rotation; Stream F `patchFlightTurnDirection` returns null on same-value no-op); Ôťů belt-and-suspenders (Stream E `parseStairField` validates via `validateStairField` ranges + `Number.isFinite` guard + CADFeedback.onError on invalid; Stream F `isStairVisibilityKey` guard + null-stair guard returning false; commit-stair listener narrows by `tool === 'stair' && action === 'commit-stair'`); Ôťů SSoT (Stream E `validateStairField` + `STAIR_FIELD_RANGES` unique source, reused by handler; `StairField` union single declaration in common-interfaces; Stream F `STAIR_RIBBON_VISIBILITY_KEYS` registry mirrors `STAIR_RIBBON_BADGE_KEYS` pattern; `getPanelVisibility` composer in useRibbonCommands routes by ownership set); Ôťů await sync (`confirmWithOverrides` is sync, `RibbonBody.filter` is sync); Ôťů explicit ownership (`useStairTool` unique listener for `commit-stair` events; `useRibbonStairBridge` unique owner of stair visibility keys; `RibbonBody` unique filter point for panel visibility). SSoT verifiche: ZERO duplicate Field union (separate StairField type, no breaking switch exhaustiveness); ZERO duplicate event payload (`DynamicSubmitDetail` extended in place, single declaration); ZERO duplicate visibility resolver (`getPanelVisibility` composed once in useRibbonCommands, used by RibbonBody); ZERO duplicate flight patch logic (`patchFlightTurnDirection` switches over discriminated union once for both flight2/3); ZERO modifiche a CanvasSection / CanvasLayerStack / canvas pipeline (ADR-040 CHECK 6B/6C/6D NON triggherano); ZERO hardcoded user-facing strings (placeholders + commands + panels all via `t(...)`, CHECK 3.8 compliant); ZERO English residue nel locale Greek. Zero `any`/`as any`/`@ts-ignore`; tutte le funzioni ÔëĄ40 lines GOL; tutti i signatures `Readonly<ÔÇŽ>` / `readonly ÔÇŽ[]`; largest file `stair-keyboard-handler.ts` ~130 LOC ÔëĄ500 (N.7.1). **Items ┬ž13 Phase 7b2a carryover resolved**: (6) Stream E Ôťů DONE; (7) Stream F Ôťů DONE. Remaining open: (i) click-on-canvas per-tread override Phase 8+; (ii) drag-to-reposition floating panel Phase 7.5+; (iii) project-scoped `dxf:project.cutPlaneHeight` setting Phase 8+. **Commit eseguito da Giorgio** (┬ž7.0). |

Numeric clamping: rise [50,300], tread [150,500], width [400,4000], stepCount round + max(2,Ôőů), storyCount round + max(1,Ôőů), storyHeight > 0. `withRecomputedTotals` ricomputa `totalRise = rise ├Ś stepCount`, `totalRun = tread ├Ś max(0, stepCount-1)`, `pitch = atan2(rise, tread) ├Ś 180/¤Ç` su rise/tread/stepCount change (UpdateStairParamsCommand.execute poi recompute anche geometry via SSoT `computeStairGeometry`). `storyCount` / `storyHeight` patch `multiStoryConfig` (default seed `{ topLevel: '', storyHeight: 2700, storyCount: 1 }` se assente). `onToggle` / `getToggleState` no-op (zero toggles in Phase 7a). **EDIT (4)** `src/subapps/dxf-viewer/app/ribbon-contextual-config.ts` ÔÇö import `CONTEXTUAL_STAIR_TAB` + `STAIR_CONTEXTUAL_TRIGGER`; ## 12. Verification (post-implementation)

- Ôťů `npm run dev` Ôćĺ DXF Viewer Ôćĺ click "╬ú╬║╬Č╬╗╬▒" Ôćĺ ogni kind disegnato correttamente.
- Ôťů Snapshot di geometria per ogni kind matches expected (visual + numeric).
- Ôťů Validator NOK respinge `rise=22cm` con messaggio greco corretto, non blocca creazione.
- Ôťů Validator hard error su `stepCount=0` blocca creazione.
- Ôťů Undo/redo creazione stair.
- Ôťů Editing post-creazione via contextual ribbon tab Ôćĺ ricalcolo geometria live.
- Ôťů Floating Advanced Properties panel apre + salva posizione.
- Ôťů Firestore: stair persiste in `floorplan_stairs` e ricarica intatta.
- Ôťů Unit tests: 100% coverage `StairGeometryService` + validator.
- Ôťů Visual regression: 10 kinds in baseline (ADR-343).
- Ôťů TypeScript: `tsc --noEmit` zero errori.
- Ôťů Pre-commit hook: 0 SSoT/i18n violations.
- Ôťů DXF export include scale come block parametrico.

### Phase 5b carryover (status post-Phase 5c)
- **Live-preview durante drag (Google-level UX)**: Phase 5b adotta commit-at-mouseUp (industry standard Revit/AutoCAD/ArchiCAD). Per per-frame preview durante drag (entity ricostruita 60├Ś/s) servirebbe un ghost-renderer su PreviewCanvas che applichi `applyStairGripDrag` ad ogni mouseMove + `computeStairGeometry(newParams)` Ôćĺ `StairRenderer.render(...)` su layer trasparente. Deferito a Phase 5d (post-validator). `computeStairGeometry` ├Ę gi├á veloce abbastanza (~ms per stair complesso) per supportare live recompute, le merging window 500 ms del `UpdateStairParamsCommand` collassano gi├á le serie di commit in 1 undo entry.
- ~~**Multi-flight grip per L/U/╬ô con angolo turn dinamico**~~: Ôťů **Phase 5c DONE 2026-05-16 (partial coverage)** ÔÇö `mirrorStairParams` con Q23 auto-flip turnDirection ora disponibile come pure function; per ╬ô flippa `turnSequence` interamente. Direction grip del flight 2/3 ESPLICITO via grip overlay resta deferito (workaround invariato: ribbon contestuale Phase 7a per `turnDirection` toggle). Phase 5c copre il caso "mirror an entire stair to flip handedness", non il caso "drag flight-2 direction grip independently".
- **Snap+ortho+polar durante drag**: l'attuale `commitDxfGripDragModeAware` riceve `delta` gi├á snapped (snap engine applica prima del commit). Verifica esplicita TBD durante visual regression Phase 6 ÔÇö se snap durante stair drag mostra inconsistency, intervenire su `useUnifiedGripInteraction.handleMouseMove` con un `snapManager.snapPoint(worldPos)` pre-`setCurrentWorldPos` (pattern gi├á usato altrove).
- **Risers / handrails / cutLine / tread labels nel renderer 2D**: Phase 5b mostra solo treads + walkline + arrow + stringers (minimal ┬ž6.2). Phase 6+ aggiunger├á il resto del pipeline ┬ž6.2 (10 layers) insieme al validator full.

### Phase 7.5 carryover (verso Phase 8+)
- **(v) ProjectId plumbing to `StairAdvancedPanelHost`** ÔÇö Phase 8 (2026-05-17) added `floorplanId?` optional prop alongside the existing `projectId?` prop, but did NOT yet plumb the actual values from `DxfViewerContent` (the caller). Until those props are wired by the caller, `useStairPersistence` no-ops internally (subscribe gated on truthy companyId/projectId/floorplanId/userId) and project-scope presets stay hidden. Next: extend `DxfViewerContent` to pass route-derived `projectId` + active `floorplanId` to `StairAdvancedPanelHost`. Trigger: caller-side wiring task (1-2 files).
- **(vi) Preset rename in-place** ÔÇö Phase 7.5 supports only Save (new) + Delete. Industry vendors (Revit Type Selector, ArchiCAD Favorites) also support rename of existing presets. Trigger: user request OR Phase 8 if Firestore persistence brings broader preset management surface.
- **(vii) Preset move between scopes** ÔÇö e.g. userÔćĺcompany promotion ("save mine as company-wide"). Industry pattern present in Revit ("Duplicate Type" + change scope). Phase 7.5 requires delete-then-resave. Trigger: user request.
- **(viii) Drag-to-reposition floating panel** ÔÇö see item (ii) Phase 7b2a carryover. Phase 7.5 ships floating panel section but does NOT add drag.
- **(ix) Optimistic UI on save** ÔÇö Phase 7.5 awaits `setDoc` before refreshing presets list. Industry latency budget ~80-150ms acceptable. Optimistic insertion (immediate visual + reconcile on confirm) deferred unless Firestore latency degrades.

### Phase 8 carryover (verso Phase 8.5 / 9+)
- **(x) Always-on subscribe** ÔÇö Phase 8 hook `useStairPersistence` is mounted by `StairAdvancedPanelHost`, which itself renders only when a stair is in primary selection. Subscribe therefore dies on deselection and resumes on next selection. This is semantically correct for "edit + persist a parametric stair" but does NOT provide always-on real-time sync of remotely-created stairs while the user is browsing the floorplan. Promote to a floor-plan-level mount (parallel to `useLevelsFirestoreSync`) when Phase 9+ adds always-on multi-user presence. Trigger: real collaborative editing requirement.
- **(xi) Full multi-user CRDT** ÔÇö Phase 8 soft-lock G24 is display-only (`editingBy` badge), not exclusivity. Two users editing the same stair simultaneously last-writer-wins on the params (selective diff-merge skips the round-trip only for the local dirty edit, not for remote conflicting edits). Industry full CRDT (Figma OT, Google Docs OT) deferred to Phase 9+. Trigger: real concurrent-edit incidents.
- **(xii) `editingBy` user name resolution** ÔÇö Soft-lock badge shows generic "╬ć╬╗╬╗╬┐¤é ¤ç¤ü╬«¤â¤ä╬Ě¤é ╬Á¤Ç╬Á╬ż╬Á¤ü╬│╬Č╬Â╬Á¤ä╬▒╬╣" ÔÇö no user lookup. Industry pattern resolves `userId Ôćĺ displayName` via contacts/users service for "Editing by MariaÔÇŽ" UX. Trigger: when a `useUserDisplayName(uid)` SSoT hook is available.
- **(xiii) Stair persistence test coverage extension** ÔÇö Phase 8 ships 19/19 service unit tests. Integration tests for `useStairPersistence` (diff-merge logic + dirty skip + lock lifecycle + debounce behavior) NOT included ÔÇö requires `renderHook` + mock `LevelManagerLike`. Trigger: regression incident OR Phase 9 collaborative-edit work.
- **(xiv) Geometry promotion to persisted `bbox` for spatial index** ÔÇö ADR ┬žG6 references "cache bbox per spatial index" but Phase 8 persists only params + validation + optional full geometry. For >100 stair per floorplan with spatial queries (Phase 9 anti-clash, BIM export), promote `bbox: { min: Point3D; max: Point3D }` to top-level `StairDoc` field with composite index. Trigger: performance degrade OR Phase 9 spatial query needs.
- **(xv) Auto-release stale locks (reader-side cleanup)** ÔÇö Phase 8 TTL is enforced ONLY by the lock-holder's own `setTimeout`. If the browser crashes, the lock persists in Firestore. Industry "reader auto-clear when `Date.now() - since.toMillis() > TTL`" deferred. Trigger: orphan-lock incidents.

### Phase 7b1 carryover (verso Phase 7b2)
- **Promotion handrail extension helpers a SSoT module** ÔÇö `pickTopExtensionMm` / `pickBottomExtensionMm` / `extendPolylineEnds` / `extendOutward` oggi locali a `StairRenderer.ts`. Se Phase 7b2 advanced panel li riusa per preview WYSIWYG (e.g. dialog di edit handrail extension live preview), promote a `src/subapps/dxf-viewer/systems/stairs/stair-handrail-render-utils.ts`. Trigger: >1 caller.
- **Promotion handrail polylines compute a `StairGeometryService`** ÔÇö oggi `StairGeometry.handrails` ├Ę popolato vuoto dalle 10 kind compute (Phase 3-4). Phase 7b1 deriva render-side da stringers, evitando l'editing di 10 file geometry. Se Phase 8 (Firestore persistence `floorplan_stairs`) richiede geometry full-cache serializzato per QTO/IFC export, allora promote compute al geometry pipeline per kind.
- **Per-kind icons split-button**: `'stair-straight'` / `'stair-spiral'` / `'stair-ushape'` icone esistono ma il ribbon home button continua ad usare `'stair'` (= straight). Phase 7.5 (library presets) o Phase 7b2 pu├▓ convertire il `draw.stair` button in split-button con variant per-kind icon.

### Phase 6 carryover (verso Phase 6.1 / 7a / 9)
- **Phase 6.1 ÔÇö wiring del `StairValidationState` allo `StairEntity.validation`**: Phase 6 espone solo la pure function `validateStairParams`. Il caller (oggi `UpdateStairParamsCommand.execute` + `useStairTool.confirm` builder Phase 5a) deve invocarla e patchare il result su `StairEntity.validation`. Plan da presentare a Giorgio prima di partire (file count + ordine commit + scelta tra (a) blocking hard-error in command `validate()`, (b) integration nel `buildStairEntity` Phase 5a, oppure (c) entrambi). Non auto-implementabile.
- ~~**Phase 6.5 ÔÇö Egress capacity validator (G20)**: `width < occupancyLoad ├Ś 7.62mm/person` warning. Type field gi├á in Phase 1 `StairParams.occupancyLoad?`. Estensione `gateStairChecker` con nuovo `checkEgress(params)` + i18n key `tools.stair.validator.egress.widthBelowOccupancy`. Project-default `occupancyLoad` (Q27) interitato; per-stair override.~~ Ôťů **Phase 6.5 DONE 2026-05-16** ÔÇö `checkEgress` aggiunto a `gate-stair-checker.ts` (universale eccetto 'none'), `validateStairParams` accetta terzo arg `projectOccupancyLoad?` (Q27 wins over per-stair override), i18n keys el+en `tools.stair.validator.egress.widthBelowOccupancy` con ICU single-brace `{occupancyLoad}`, 8 nuovi test.
- ~~**Phase 6.5 ÔÇö ADA handrail extensions RENDER + auto-default**: type fields `topExtension` / `bottomExtension` gi├á Phase 1; validator Phase 6 Ôťů; RENDER (305mm top horizontal extension + one-tread bottom extension polyline) deferito a `StairRenderer` estensione + auto-default Phase 5a builder quando `codeProfile==='ada'` (Q26 pacchetto coherent).~~ **PARZIALMENTE DONE Phase 6.5 2026-05-16** ÔÇö auto-default builder `buildDefaultStairParams` con `codeProfile='ada'` ora auto-applica `handrails.topExtension=305` + `bottomExtension='one-tread'` + `adaContrastStrip=true` + `handrails.height=900` (mid-range ADA [864, 965]) tramite helper `buildHandrails(codeProfile, override?)`; caller overrides preservati per-field. **RENDER spostato a Phase 7a** ÔÇö vedi entry sotto.
- **Phase 7a ÔÇö ADA handrail extensions RENDER (deferred from Phase 6.5)**: il render `StairRenderer` delle 305mm top horizontal extension + one-tread bottom polyline ├Ę spostato a Phase 7a per coherent visual pacchetto con red-badge UI surfacing. Rationale: (1) Phase 5b ┬ž6.2 lascia esplicitamente `StairRenderer` minimal ("no handrails, no risers, no cutLine zigzag") con il pipeline 10-layer in progressive ship a Phase 6+ generale; (2) senza red-badge UI surfacing nello stesso ship visual, il render handrail extensions non ha contesto di feedback per validation; (3) safer split ÔÇö Phase 6.5 data layer ├Ę zero-visual-regression. Phase 7a aggiunger├á: handrail polyline base (inner/outer) + ADA top extension 305mm horizontal nella direction del top tread + ADA bottom one-tread extension nella direction del bottom tread + dashed stroke style.
- **Phase 9 ÔÇö 3D headroom raycast**: cheap 2D proxy Phase 6 usa `clearance = ceiling.elevation Ôłĺ (basePoint.z + totalRise)` come approssimazione conservativa. Phase 9 implementa raycast per-step (vertical ray dall'apice di ogni nosing verso `+Z` fino al primo hit ceiling/slab/roof) ÔÇö required per overhanging ceilings + multi-flight stairs con landing intermediate.

=======
### Phase 5c carryover (verso Phase 5c.1 / 6 / 7a)
- **Branch standard Mirror/Rotate/Move commands per type==='stair'**: Phase 5c espone solo le pure functions `mirrorStairParams`/`rotateStairParams`/`copyStairParams`. I comandi standard `MirrorEntityCommand` (`core/commands/entity-commands/MirrorEntityCommand.ts`), `RotateEntityCommand`, `MoveEntityCommand` operano oggi via `mirrorEntity`/`rotateEntity`/translation diretta sulle vertices raw ÔÇö se invocati su una stair romperebbero la parametricit├á (Revit bug noto). Phase 5c.1 deve introdurre un branch `type === 'stair'` in ciascuno dei tre comandi che dispatcha alle pure transforms + recompute `geometry` via `computeStairGeometry` (pattern identico a `UpdateStairParamsCommand` Phase 5b). Plan da presentare a Giorgio prima di partire (file count + ordine commit), non auto-implementabile.
- **Live-preview durante mirror/rotate/copy interattivo**: stessa nota della Phase 5b live-preview (deferito Phase 5d).
- **Rotate(180┬░) === Mirror semantics check**: Q23 nota che "rotate 180┬░ comporta stesso flip semantico del mirror" ÔÇö Phase 5c implementa rotate SENZA flip di turnDirection (rotation preserva la chiralit├á, a differenza di reflection). La nota Q23 va interpretata come UX expectation ("180┬░ rotate visivamente equivale a mirror"), NON come obbligo di flip turnDirection. Coerenza con industry (Revit/ArchiCAD/AutoCAD Arch: rotate non flippa handedness). Da confermare a Giorgio durante demo Phase 5c.1 se l'aspettativa UX ├Ę diversa.
